weeks</td> <td>○ No certificates</td> </tr> </tbody> </table> </div> <h3 id="basic">Basic Courses</h3> <p>Currently, CS50 offers two basic courses. These can be seen as optional on-ramps to CS50’s core courses. If you don’t feel ready for a formal introduction to computer science, this is a good place to start.</p> <h4 id="CS50T"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-understanding-technology-10142">CS50&#8217;s Understanding Technology (CS50T)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-71606 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-1024x481.png" alt="CS50’s Understanding Technology" width="1024" height="481" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-1024x481.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-300x141.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-768x361.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429-1536x722.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/Screenshot-from-2020-05-19-18-28-41-e1589907389429.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50T is a gentle introduction to the world of computing. It starts at the hardware level and works its way up from there. It explores how the internet works, how websites are created, and how security is ensured. And it ends with coding basics.</p> <p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 4 hours of study per week over 6 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/technology">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-understanding-technology-10142">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li><a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/1a">Paid transcript and academic credit</a> via Harvard Extension School</li> </ul> <p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-cs50-ap-computer-science-principles-21947">XSeries program in CS50&#8217;s AP Computer Science Principles</a>.</p> <h4 id="CS50S"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-scratch-39309">CS50&#8217;s Introduction to Programming with Scratch (CS50S)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-76346 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s.png" alt="" width="1024" height="481" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s-300x141.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50s-768x361.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50S is a gentle introduction to programming. It focuses on Scratch, a language that makes coding highly visual. Instead of typing text, you combine functional blocks as if they were LEGO pieces to create programs. The course covers all programming fundamentals, including variables, functions, and loops.</p> <p>The course is taught by <a href="https://brianyu.me/">Brian Yu</a>. It involves about 6 hours of study per week over 3 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/scratch/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-scratch-39309">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> </ul> <h3 id="core">Core Courses</h3> <p>Currently, CS50 offers three core courses. These include the original CS50 as well as variants geared toward different types of learners. This is where most learners want to start. One course should be plenty. But learners that take a variant may want to also take the original CS50 — especially if they plan to continue with a follow-up course.</p> <h4 id="CS50"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-computer-science-442">CS50 Introduction to Computer Science</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-84537" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/05/cs50-2023-student-demo-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50 is Harvard’s computer science introduction. It starts with binary and goes up the ladder of abstraction from machine code to low-level languages to high-level languages. It explores algorithms, data structures, and memory management. And it ends with one of three specialization tracks: web, game, or mobile development.</p> <p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 12 hours of study per week over 12 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/x">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-computer-science-442">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li>Paid transcript and academic credit via <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/50">Harvard Extension School</a> or <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/summer/csci/s/50">Harvard Summer School</a></li> </ul> <p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s professional certificates:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-web-programming-18465">Computer Science for Web Programming</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-artifical-intellige-18468">Computer Science for Artificial Intelligence</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-game-development-18456">Computer Science for Game Development</a></li> </ul> <p>If you&#8217;d like to learn more, I&#8217;ve written a dedicated article on the course: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/cs50-free-certificate/">Harvard CS50 in 2023: How to Get a Free Certificate</a>.</p> <h4 id="CS50L"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-for-lawyers-16857">CS50’s Computer Science for Lawyers (CS50L)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-71611" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-1024x479.png" alt="CS50 for lawyers" width="1024" height="479" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-1024x479.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50lawfinal.png 1180w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50L is a CS50 variant geared toward lawyers and law students. Part of the curriculum explores similar content but emphasizes big-picture understanding over low-level details. The other part explores entirely new content that considers how law and computer science interact — for instance, in regards to cybersecurity, data privacy, and internet regulation.</p> <p>The course is taught by David J. Malan and <a href="https://douglloyd.com/">Doug Lloyd</a>. It involves about 4 hours of study per week over 10 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/law/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-for-lawyers-16857">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li><a href="https://hls.harvard.edu/executive-education/programs/online-programs/computer-science-for-lawyers/">Paid certificate</a> via Harvard Law School Executive Education</li> </ul> <h4 id="CS50B"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-computer-science-for-business-professionals-10143">CS50&#8217;s Computer Science for Business Professionals (CS50B)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71610 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 Business" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50b-e1589908163415.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50B is a CS50 variant geared toward business professionals. Most of the course explores similar content but emphasizes big-picture understanding over low-level details. A small part explores entirely new content relevant to businesses — for instance, cloud computing.</p> <p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 4 hours of study per week over 6 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/business/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-computer-science-for-business-professionals-10143">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li>Paid transcript and academic credit via <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/1b">Harvard Extension School</a> or <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/summer/csci/s/1b">Harvard Summer School</a></li> </ul> <h4 id="CS50P"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-python-58275">CS50&#8217;s Introduction to Programming with Python (CS50P)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-78729" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python.png" alt="" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/09/cs50-python-768x359.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50P teaches the fundamentals of programming in Python, including variables, functions, loops, and reading and writing files. It draws from real-world programming problems and has plenty of practical exercises.</p> <p>The course is taught by David J. Malan. It involves about 6 hours of study per week over 9 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/python">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/cs50s-introduction-to-programming-with-python-58275">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li><a href="https://courses.dce.harvard.edu/?details&amp;srcdb=202301&amp;crn=15376">Paid transcript and academic credit</a> via Harvard Extension School (taught by Jeff Parker)</li> </ul> <p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-python-programming-98208">Professional Certificate in Computer Science for Python Programming</a>.</p> <p>If you&#8217;d like to learn more, I&#8217;ve written a dedicated article on the course: <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/harvard-cs50-python/">Harvard New Intro to Python: How to Earn a Free Certificate</a>.</p> <h3 id="followup">Follow-Up Courses</h3> <p>Currently, CS50 offers five follow-up courses. These pick up where CS50 leaves off and explore a specific subject. They&#8217;re an excellent way to build on your computer science fundamentals by delving into a specialization.</p> <h4 id="CS50AI"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-artificial-intelligence-with-python-18122">CS50’s Introduction to Artificial Intelligence with Python (CS50AI)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71612 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 AI" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50ai-e1589908343841.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50AI leverages the Python programming language to explore modern artificial intelligence. It covers foundational AI concepts, such as search algorithms and knowledge models, and builds on them to discuss more advanced concepts, such as optimization and machine learning.</p> <p>The course is taught by <a href="https://brianyu.me/">Brian Yu</a>. It involves about 20 hours of study per week over 7 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/ai/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-artificial-intelligence-with-python-18122">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li>Paid transcript and academic credit via <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/80">Harvard Extension School</a> or <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/summer/csci/s/80">Harvard Summer School</a></li> </ul> <p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-artifical-intellige-18468">Professional Certificate in Computer Science for Artificial Intelligence</a>.</p> <h4 id="CS50W"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-web-programming-with-python-and-javascript-11506">CS50’s Web Programming with Python and JavaScript (CS50W)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50webfinal.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone size-large wp-image-71613" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50webfinal-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 Web Development" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50webfinal-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50webfinal-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50webfinal-768x358.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50webfinal.png 1181w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50W explores the languages, tools, and processes underpinning modern web app development. It covers languages such as Python and JavaScript, frameworks such as Flask and Django, and services such as GitHub and Heroku.</p> <p>The course is taught by <a href="https://brianyu.me/">Brian Yu</a>. It involves about 8 hours of study per week over 12 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/web/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-web-programming-with-python-and-javascript-11506">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li>Paid transcript and academic credit via <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/33a">Harvard Extension School</a> or <a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/summer/csci/s/33a">Harvard Summer School</a></li> </ul> <p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-web-programming-18465">Professional Certificate in Computer Science for Web Programming</a>.</p> <h4 id="CS50G"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-game-development-11504">CS50&#8217;s Introduction to Game Development (CS50G)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71614 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game-e1589908765679-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 Game Development" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game-e1589908765679-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game-e1589908765679-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game-e1589908765679-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game-e1589908765679-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50game-e1589908765679.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50G explores the languages, tools, and processes underpinning modern game development. It leverages languages such as C# and frameworks such as Unity to create 2D and 3D experiences, and draws examples from video games such as Pong, Mario, and Portal.</p> <p>The course is taught by <a href="https://github.com/coltonoscopy">Colton Ogden</a>. It involves about 8 hours of study per week over 12 weeks. And it offers the following certificate options:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/games/">Free certificate</a> via Harvard OpenCourseWare</li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-introduction-to-game-development-11504">Paid verified certificate</a> via edX</li> <li><a href="https://web.dce.harvard.edu/extension/csci/e/23a">Paid transcript and academic credit</a> via Harvard Extension School</li> </ul> <p>The course is also part of edX&#8217;s <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/harvardx-computer-science-for-game-development-18456">Professional Certificate in Computer Science for Game Development</a>.</p> <h4 id="CS50M"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/course/edx-cs50-s-mobile-app-development-with-react-native-11505">CS50&#8217;s Mobile App Development with React Native (CS50M)</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71615 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367-1024x478.png" alt="CS50 Mobile App Development" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50mobile-e1589908823367.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50M explores how to develop mobile apps using the React Native framework. It covers concepts such as state and components, processes such as testing and deployment, and tools such as Redux and JSX.</p> <p>The course is taught by Jordan Hayashi. It involves about 8 hours of study per week over 13 weeks. And it is offered via <a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/mobile/">Harvard OpenCourseWare</a> but has no certificate.</p> <h4 id="CS50Beyond"><a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/beyond/">CS50 Beyond</a></h4> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond.png"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-71616 size-large" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond-e1589908890517-1024x478.png" alt="" width="1024" height="478" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond-e1589908890517-1024x478.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond-e1589908890517-300x140.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond-e1589908890517-768x359.png 768w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond-e1589908890517-1536x718.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2020/05/cs50beyond-e1589908890517.png 1920w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <p>CS50 Beyond is the precursor of CS50W. It explores the same subject, web development, but does it in a more condensed time frame. Most topics remain the same but most projects are different.</p> <p>The course is taught by <a href="https://brianyu.me/">Brian Yu</a>. It involves about 5 hours of study per week over 12 weeks. And it is offered via <a href="https://cs50.harvard.edu/beyond/">Harvard OpenCourseWare</a> but has no certificate.</p> <p>The post <a rel="nofollow" सर्वश्रेष्ठ पाठ्यक्रम मार्गदर्शिकाएँ हत्तपः://ववव.क्लाससेंट्रल.कॉम/रिपोर्ट/?प=85198 <p>यहां सीएसएस एनिमेशन सीखने के लिए सर्वोत्तम ऑनलाइन पाठ्यक्रमों के साथ एक गाइड है, वेब एनीमेशन बनाने का पसंदीदा तरीका, इसके प्रदर्शन, सरलता, पहुंच और ब्राउज़र समर्थन को देखते हुए।</p> <p>पोस्ट <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-css-animation-courses/">2023 में लेने के लिए 10 सर्वश्रेष्ठ CSS एनिमेशन कोर्स</a> सबसे पहले <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">द क्लास सेंट्रल की रिपोर्ट</a> पर दिखाई दिया।</p> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-85203 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/CSS-Animation-BCG-Banner.png" alt="" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/CSS-Animation-BCG-Banner.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/CSS-Animation-BCG-Banner-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2023/02/CSS-Animation-BCG-Banner-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p> <p>So, you have finished a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/best-web-development-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">web development course</a> teaching you HTML and CSS with a small section on CSS Animations that got you extremely excited. You are now wondering: “Where can I learn more about animations and bring life to my next project?”</p> <p>While searching for CSS Animation, I could hardly find tutorials and wondered if there were people like me, who were stuck looking for Animation tutorials without Javascript. Javascript is great and can be used for complex animations but that requires learning a new programming language again and I just wanted to make subtle animations to make my project more dynamic and engaging.</p> <p>So, here are a few of my top picks to learn CSS Animation. With CSS, you can animate elements with a few lines of code, whereas JavaScript animations require more complex logic and code.</li> <li aria-level="1">Accessibility: CSS Animations can be controlled with CSS and are accessible to users with assistive technologies, such as screen readers. JavaScript animations, on the other hand, may not be accessible to all users.</li> <li aria-level="1">Browser support: CSS Animations have good browser support, meaning they work on most modern browsers. This is not always the case with JavaScript animations, as some browsers may not support certain JavaScript features.</li> </ol> <p>So, let’s learn some Animation with CSS.</p> <p><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-79247 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png" alt="Find your next course." width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/03/Class-Central-Preview-1-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a></p> <h2>Best Courses Guides Methodology</h2> <p>I built this ranking following the now tried-and-tested methodology used in previous Best Courses Guides (<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/category/best-courses/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">you can find them all here</a>). 2023 13:45:13 +0000 गाइड चीन एक्स यूई डॉन एक्स हत्तपः://ववव.क्लाससेंट्रल.कॉम/रिपोर्ट/?प=69630 <p>चीन में ऑनलाइन शिक्षा जीवित और अच्छी तरह से है। संयुक्त रूप से, ये प्लेटफ़ॉर्म 100K से अधिक ऑनलाइन पाठ्यक्रम प्रदान करते हैं।</p> <p>पोस्ट <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/chinese-mooc-platforms/">2023 में चीनी ऑनलाइन कोर्स प्लैटफ़ॉर्म की व्यापक सूची</a> पहली बार दिखाई दी <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">क्लास सेंट्रल की रिपोर्ट</a> पर।</p> <p><img loading="lazy" class="alignnone wp-image-73877 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms.png" alt="Chinese Language MOOC Platforms" width="1024" height="512" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2021/01/chinese-lang-platforms-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></p> <p>The origins of <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/help/moocs" target="_blank" rel="noopener">massive open online courses</a> (MOOCs) in China can be traced back to <a href="https://pdfs.semanticscholar.org/07ff/a996d12fff4691ead559912a41cdf31d54b3.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">November 2011</a>, when <a href="http://www.chinadaily.com.cn/cndy/2011-11/10/content_14068582.htm" target="_blank" rel="noopener">20 courses</a> from Chinese universities were made available online through the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OpenCourseWare" target="_blank" rel="noopener">OpenCourseWare</a> platform <a href="http://www.icourses.cn/home/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">iCourse</a>.</p> <p>For years at <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/">Class Central</a>, we&#8217;ve been interested in the development of online education in China. You can find our <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/tag/china/">coverage on the subject here</a>.</p> <p>In this article, we discuss the emergence of MOOCs in China and compile a comprehensive list of Chinese-language online course platforms.</p> <h2>Origins</h2> <p>The first full-fledged MOOC platform in China, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">XuetangX</a>, was launched in October 2013 by <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/university/tsu" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tsinghua University</a>. Many more similar platforms would promptly follow.</p> <p>Like <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/mooc-platforms/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">online course platforms worldwide</a>, Chinese MOOC platforms saw a <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/the-second-year-of-the-mooc/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">surge</a> in both <a href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/08dMP3NQXSqTXznRajBsmw" target="_blank" rel="noopener">course numbers and enrollments</a> in 2020 due to the pandemic.</p> <p>In <strong>early 2022</strong>, the Chinese platforms listed in this article offered close to <strong>70K</strong> online courses. That&#8217;s about twice as many as in 2020. Now, in <strong>early 2023</strong>, we reached a total of about <strong>100K</strong> courses, showing that the growth trend perdures.</p> <p>On March 28, 2022, China’s Ministry of Education announced the “<a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-integrated-platforms/">Smart Education of China</a>” initiative and launched the comprehensive website <a href="https://www.chinaooc.com.cn/">Chinaooc</a>, bringing together all the MOOC platforms of mainland China.</p> <h2>Platforms</h2> <p>Here are the Chinese online course platforms that focus on MOOCs. You can click on one to jump to the description.</p> <ul> <li><a href="#XuetangX">XuetangX</a></li> <li><a href="#Chinese-University-MOOC">Chinese University MOOC</a></li> <li><a style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85163" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped.png" alt="" width="1536" height="854" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/xuetangx-homepage-2023-cropped.png 1536w, id="caption-attachment-85163" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.xuetangx.com/">XuetangX homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>In October 2013, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/university/tsu" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Tsinghua University</a> along with partner institutions in China <a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20200804053937/https://www.edx.org/press/edx-open-source-platform-chosen-power" target="_blank" rel="noopener">announced</a> the launch of XuetangX, China’s first MOOC platform. The are close to <a href="https://www.xuetangx.com/search">7000 courses</a> and programs offered on the platform, including live streamings, online degrees, microcredentials, and cohort-based boot camps. XuetangX reached over <a href="https://mp.weixin.qq.com/s/an4guDM-tEFz4Vn7Bs_pZA" target="_blank" rel="noopener">80 million</a> users at its 8th anniversary on October 10, 2021.</p> <p>The platform raised <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx-raises-funding-drops-open-edx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">series B funding</a>, moved away from Open edX and <a href="https://next.xuetangx.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">redesigned</a> their website at the beginning of 2020. In April 2020, <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-mooc-platforms-go-international/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">it went international</a> and began to offer around 470 free English courses for global learners.</p> <p>Here&#8217;s some of Class Central&#8217;s previous coverage on XuetangX:</p> <ul> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx-raises-funding-drops-open-edx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">XuetangX Raises Series B Funding, Moves Away From Open edX Platform</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-mooc-platforms-go-international/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">China’s Largest MOOC Platforms Go International, Launch Courses in English</a></li> <li><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/xuetangx/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">XuetangX: A Look at China’s First and Biggest MOOC Platform</a></li> </ul> <h2 id="Chinese-University-MOOC">Chinese University MOOC</h2> <figure id="attachment_85167" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85167" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final.png"><img loading="lazy" class="size-full wp-image-85167" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final.png" alt="" width="1536" height="767" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final-1024x511.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icourse-homepage-2023-cropped-final-768x384.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85167" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.icourse163.org/">iCourse homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>Chinese University MOOC, also often called <a href="https://www.icourse163.org/">iCourse</a>, is the fruit of a collaboration between the Chinese internet giant NetEase and the original <a href="http://www.icourses.cn/home/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">iCourse learning platform</a>. The MOOC platform offers over 10,000 free university courses, including <a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/china-national-moocs/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">nationally-recognized MOOCs</a>. Free digital certificates are automatically available when students pass quizzes and final exam.</p> <h2 id="Zhihuishu">Zhihui Shu</h2> <figure id="attachment_85169" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85169" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85169 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="791" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023-300x154.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023-1024x527.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/zhihuishu-homepage-2023-768x396.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85169" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/">Zhihui Shu homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/">Zhihui Shu</a>, which translates to “Wisdom Tree”, was launched in <a href="https://www.google.com/books/edition/_/T5xBDwAAQBAJ?hl=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener">December 2012</a>. It has the particularity of allowing its university partners to share credit-bearing courses with one another, facilitating academic credit mobility across China.</p> <p>Of the 14,100 courses offered on the platform, 10,500 (that is, 75%) are credit-granting courses only for on-campus students. The platform offers <a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/portals_h5/2clearning.html#/courseResource/?type=3&amp;label=-1&amp;payState=0&amp;interestSort=1" target="_blank" rel="noopener">45</a> courses with a free digital certificates. And there are also <a href="https://www.zhihuishu.com/columnsapp/student/microSpecialtyMore.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">18 microcredential programs</a> available.</p> <h2 id="CNMOOC">CNMOOC</h2> <figure id="attachment_85171" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85171" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85171 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="991" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023-300x194.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023-1024x661.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/CNMOOC-homepage-2023-768x496.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85171" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.cnmooc.org/">CNMOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>In April 2014, Shanghai Jiao Tong University launched <a href="https://www.cnmooc.org/">CNMOOC</a>, a online course platform promoting the integration of MOOCs into China’s on-campus higher education system. The platform offers over <a href="https://www.cnmooc.org/portal/frontCourseIndex/course.mooc" target="_blank" rel="noopener">3000</a> courses. About half of them provide free digital certificates.</p> <h2 id="Xue-Yin-Online">Xue Yin Online</h2> <figure id="attachment_85172" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85172" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85172 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="698" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023-300x136.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023-1024x465.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Xue-Yin-Online-homepage-2023-768x349.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85172" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.xueyinonline.com/">Xue Yin Online homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://www.xueyinonline.com/">Xue Yin Online</a> launched in November 2017. It was developed by The Open University of China and the Chaoxing Group. The purpose of this online course platform is to serve as a “credit bank” for vocational skills, facilitating the transfer of credit and the recognition of prior learning across different universities. The platform offers nearly over <a href="http://www.xueyinonline.com/mooc/courselist" target="_blank" rel="noopener">16,000</a> course with a free digital certificate.</p> <h2 id="Chinese-MOOCs">Chinese MOOCs</h2> <figure id="attachment_85174" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85174" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85174 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="557" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023-300x109.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023-1024x371.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/chinese-moocs-homepage-2023-768x279.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85174" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/">Chinese MOOCs</a> homepage in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/">Chinese MOOCs</a> was founded in <a href="https://www.google.com/books/edition/_/T5xBDwAAQBAJ?hl=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener">February 2015</a> by Peking University in collaboration with the Alibaba Group. About <a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/kvideo.php?do=search" target="_blank" rel="noopener">150 free courses</a> with a <a href="http://www.chinesemooc.org/do.php?ac=helpCenter" target="_blank" rel="noopener">free digital certificate</a> are offered on the platform, most of them provided by Peking University.</p> <h2 id="UOOC-Online">UOOC Online</h2> <figure id="attachment_85175" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85175" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85175 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="829" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023-300x162.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023-1024x553.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/uooc-online-homepage-2023-768x415.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85175" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.uooconline.com/">UOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>The <a href="http://www.uooconline.com/">University Open Online Courses</a> (UOOC) platform was founded by Shenzhen University in February 2016, subsuming the preexisting MOOC platform from <a href="http://www.suda.edu.cn/eng/News/SoochowNews/201611/AE0FB5A2-FBE4-4116-85BE-A14E3FE2307E.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">April 2014</a>. The are <a href="http://www.uooconline.com/course/list" target="_blank" rel="noopener">1375</a> free courses on the platform, with the vast majority also offering credit for on-campus students.</p> <h2 id="Zhejiang-Provincial-MOOC-Platform">Zhejiang Provincial MOOC Platform</h2> <figure id="attachment_85176" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85176" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85176 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="797" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023-300x156.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023-1024x531.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/Zhejiang-online-homepage-2023-768x399.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85176" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.zjooc.cn/">Zhejiang Provincial MOOC Platform homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>The Zhejiang Institutions of Higher Learning Online Open Course Sharing Platform — or <a href="https://www.zjooc.cn/">Zhejiang Provincial MOOC Platform</a> for short — is backed by the Education Department of the province of Zhejiang, south of Shanghai. There are <a href="https://www.zjooc.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">17,500</a> courses offered on the platform.</p> <h2 id="E-Huixue">E-Huixue</h2> <figure id="attachment_85177" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85177" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85177 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="957" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023-300x187.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023-1024x638.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/e-huixue-homepage-2023-768x479.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85177" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.ehuixue.cn/">E-Huixue homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>In December 2015, the Department of Education of the Aihui District, situated in the northwest of China, launched <a href="http://www.ehuixue.cn/">E-Huixue</a>. Like Zhejiang’s Provincial MOOC Platform, the purpose of E-Huixue is to serve as a regional repository for online courses. The platform offers more than <a href="https://www.ehuixue.cn/index/clist/index.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2500</a> MOOCs with a free digital certificate.</p> <h2 id="CQOOC">CQOOC</h2> <figure id="attachment_85178" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85178" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85178 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="899" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023-300x176.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023-1024x599.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/cqooc-homepage-2023-768x450.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85178" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.cqooc.com/">CQOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://www.cqooc.com/">Chongqing University Open Online Learning Platform</a> (CQOOC), was established by the Ministry of Education in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chongqing" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Chongqing</a> (a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Direct-administered_municipalities_of_China" target="_blank" rel="noopener">municipality</a> in southwest China) in June 2016. Around <a href="http://www.cqooc.com/course?el=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4300</a> courses, mostly from universities and colleges in Chongqing, are offered on the platform.</p> <h2 id="Rong-You-Xue-Tang">Rong You Xue Tang</h2> <figure id="attachment_85179" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85179" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85179 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1024" height="532" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023-300x156.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/rong-homepage-2023-768x399.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85179" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.livedu.com.cn/ispace4.0/moocMainIndex/mainIndex.do">Rong You Xue Tang homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p>Rong You Xue Tang is the new name of the former Beijing MOOC Research Association platform. It was founded in 2016 by Renmin University of China together with several Beijing-based universities. Over <a href="http://www.livedu.com.cn/ispace4.0/moocxjkc/queryAllKc.do" target="_blank" rel="noopener">210 free courses</a> are provided on the platform, some of which are <a href="https://www.livedu.com.cn/ispace4.0/moocXwwh/moocqueryXwByid?xwid=AE50F17B26C8EC2FE050007F0100194F" target="_blank" rel="noopener">credit-eligible</a> courses.</p> <h2 id="Ulearning">Ulearning</h2> <figure id="attachment_85180" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85180" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85180 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="797" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023-300x156.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023-1024x531.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ulearning-homepage-2023-768x399.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85180" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.ulearning.cn/portal/index.html#/index/portal">Ulearning homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://www.ulearning.cn/portal/index.html#/index/portal">Ulearning</a> was launched by the online learning company <a href="http://www.ulearning.com.cn/about_profiles.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Ulearning</a> in May 2015. There are close to <a href="https://www.ulearning.cn/portal/index.html#/index/openCourse" target="_blank" rel="noopener">2700</a> courses provided on the platform.</p> <h2 id="ICVE-MOOC-College">ICVE MOOC College</h2> <figure id="attachment_85181" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85181" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85181 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="982" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023-300x192.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023-1024x655.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ivce-homepage-2023-768x491.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85181" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://icve-mooc.icve.com.cn/">ICVE homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://icve-mooc.icve.com.cn/">ICVE</a> was built for professional education by <a href="http://www.hep.com.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Higher Education Press</a> in 2014. There are over <a href="https://icve-mooc.icve.com.cn/cms/moocCourse/index.htm">7300</a> free courses offered on the platform, and over 80% of them provide a free certificate.</p> <h2 id="ICC">ICC</h2> <figure id="attachment_85182" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85182" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85182 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="982" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023-300x192.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023-1024x655.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/icc-homepage-2023-768x491.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85182" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://icc.hep.com.cn/">ICC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://icc.hep.com.cn/">ICC</a> was launched by <a href="http://www.hep.com.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Higher Education Press</a> in 2016. More than <a href="https://icc.hep.com.cn/homeAllCourse.action" target="_blank" rel="noopener">4000</a> courses from <a href="https://icc.hep.com.cn/homeAllSchool.action" target="_blank" rel="noopener">210</a> universities are offered on the platform.</p> <h2 id="ErYa">ErYa</h2> <figure id="attachment_85183" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85183" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85183 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="805" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023-300x157.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023-1024x537.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ErYa-homepage-2023-768x403.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85183" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://erya.mooc.chaoxing.com/">ErYa homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://erya.mooc.chaoxing.com/">ErYa</a> was launched in January 2015 by the Chaoxing Group, an edtech corporation based in Beijing. The MOOC platform offers around <a href="http://erya.mooc.chaoxing.com/engine2/general/more?t=74115A8FB97F7D0818B962CED639690CD719A9A2BD60988D17620715E89547CEB516A82E93540ECA5645E68AE76744E2">500</a> free courses in liberal arts from humanities to creative thinking.</p> <h2 id="gaoxiaobang">Gaoxiaobang</h2> <figure id="attachment_85184" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85184" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85184 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="766" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023-300x150.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023-1024x511.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/gaoxiaobang-homepage-2023-768x383.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85184" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://imooc.gaoxiaobang.com/">Gaoxiaobang homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://imooc.gaoxiaobang.com/">Gaoxiaobang</a> was established by a subsidiary of <a href="https://www.huike.com/index" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Huike Group</a>, a company focused on the upskilling and reskilling of professionals in tech-related domains. The platform was launched in September 2015, and it currently offers close to <a href="https://imooc.gaoxiaobang.com/#/courses" target="_blank" rel="noopener">470</a> free courses.</p> <h2 id="PMPHMOOC">PMPHMOOC</h2> <figure id="attachment_85185" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85185" style="width: 1024px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85185 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1024" height="528" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023-300x155.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/PMPHMOOC-homepage-2023-768x396.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1024px) 100vw, 1024px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85185" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.pmphmooc.com/">PMPHMOOC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://www.pmphmooc.com/">PMPHMOOC</a> was established in 2015 by the medical publisher <a href="https://www.pmph.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">People’s Medical Publishing House</a> in partnership with medical schools and academic institutions across China. It provides <a href="http://www.pmphmooc.com/mooc_system/#/moocIndex">70 health-related MOOCs</a> in 10 subjects — for instance, in anatomy and biochemistry.</p> <h2 id="UMOOCs">UMOOCs</h2> <figure id="attachment_85186" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85186" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85186 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="733" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023-300x143.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023-1024x489.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/umoocs-homepage-2023-768x367.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85186" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://moocs.unipus.cn/">UMOOCs homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://moocs.unipus.cn/">UMOOCs</a> is a Chinese MOOC platform for studying foreign languages. The platform was founded by Beijing Foreign Studies University in December 2017, and it is affiliated with the Foreign Language Teaching and Research Press, a publishing company dedicated to all facets of foreign language study in China. It offers over <a href="http://moocs.unipus.cn/course/explore" target="_blank" rel="noopener">400 free courses with certificate</a> covering 10 languages.</p> <h2 id="iLab-X">iLab-X</h2> <figure id="attachment_85187" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85187" style="width: 1536px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85187 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1536" height="772" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023.png 1536w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023-300x151.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023-1024x515.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ilabx-homepage-2023-768x386.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1536px) 100vw, 1536px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85187" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.ilab-x.com/">iLab-X homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://www.ilab-x.com/">iLab-X</a> is a MOOC platform for virtual simulation experiments launched by <a href="http://www.hep.com.cn/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Higher Education Press</a> in 2017. Close to <a href="http://www.ilab-x.com/list" target="_blank" rel="noopener">3500</a> virtual experiments are provided on the platform.</p> <h2 id="MOEC">MOEC</h2> <figure id="attachment_85188" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85188" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85188 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="964" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023-300x188.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023-1024x642.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/moec-homepage-2023-768x482.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85188" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/">MOEC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/">MOEC</a> is a MOOC platform for virtual simulation experiment education in medicine, launched by the company <a href="http://www.mengoo.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Mengoo</a> in 2020. The MOOC platform has provided around <a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/curriculum.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">720</a> courses in medicine for over <a href="https://yxsypt.com/training/manage/portal/cooperativeUniversity.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener">100</a> university medical schools in China.</p> <h2 id="Educoder">Educoder</h2> <figure id="attachment_85189" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85189" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85189 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="641" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023-300x125.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023-1024x427.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/educoder-homepage-2023-768x320.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85189" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.educoder.net/">MOEC homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://www.educoder.net/">Educoder</a> is a MOOC platform for computer science and programming that was launched in July 2016. There are over <a href="https://www.educoder.net/paths" target="_blank" rel="noopener">640</a> free courses and thousands of free programming exercises. The MOOC platform also allows its verified users to create their own courses, exercises, and <a href="https://www.educoder.net/classrooms" target="_blank" rel="noopener">online classrooms</a>.</p> <h2 id="eWant">eWant</h2> <figure id="attachment_85190" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85190" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85190 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="644" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023-300x126.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023-1024x429.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/ewant-homepage-2023-768x322.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85190" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="http://www.ewant.org/">eWant homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="http://www.ewant.org/">eWant</a> is a MOOC platform that was launched by National Chiao Tung University in 2013. National Chiao Tung University is one of Taiwan’s leading public research universities, located in Hsinchu, Taiwan. It hosts more than <a href="https://www.ewant.org/admin/tool/mooccourse/allcourses.php" target="_blank" rel="noopener">3200</a> courses from over <a href="https://www.ewant.org/local/school/list.php?lang=en" target="_blank" rel="noopener">90</a> different universities.</p> <h2 id="ShareCourse">ShareCourse</h2> <figure id="attachment_85191" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85191" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85191 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="859" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023-300x168.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023-1024x572.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/sharecourse-homepage-2023-768x429.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85191" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/">ShareCourse homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/">ShareCourse</a> was founded by Taiwan’s National Tsing Hua University in <a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/sharecourse/general/home/aboutUs" target="_blank" rel="noopener">September 2012</a>. 90 institutions contributed over <a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/sharecourse/course/view/searchCourse/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">650</a> courses to the MOOC platform. About <a href="https://www.sharecourse.net/sharecourse/course/view/categorySearch/6/23?type=2" target="_blank" rel="noopener">190</a> of them are free.</p> <h2 id="OpenEdu">OpenEdu</h2> <figure id="attachment_85192" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-85192" style="width: 1537px" class="wp-caption alignnone"><a href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/openedu-homepage-2023.png"><img loading="lazy" class="wp-image-85192 size-full" src="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/openedu-homepage-2023.png" alt="" width="1537" height="832" srcset="https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/openedu-homepage-2023.png 1537w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/openedu-homepage-2023-300x162.png 300w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/openedu-homepage-2023-1024x554.png 1024w, https://www.classcentral.com/report/wp-content/uploads/2022/01/openedu-homepage-2023-768x416.png 768w" sizes="(max-width: 1537px) 100vw, 1537px" /></a><figcaption id="caption-attachment-85192" class="wp-caption-text"><a href="https://www.openedu.tw/">OpenEdu homepage</a> in 2023</figcaption></figure> <p><a href="https://www.openedu.tw/">OpenEdu</a> is a MOOC platform from Taiwan. The MOOC platform is based on Open edX and offers over <a href="https://www.openedu.tw/search" target="_blank" rel="noopener">470</a> courses in subjects including computer science, business management, humanities and art.</p> <p>The post <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report/chinese-mooc-platforms/">Massive List of Chinese Online Course Platforms in 2023</a> appeared first on <a rel="nofollow" href="https://www.classcentral.com/report">The Report by Class Central</a>.</p> हत्तपः://ववव.क्लाससेंट्रल.कॉम/रिपोर्ट/चिनेसे-मूक-प्लेटफॉर्म्स/फीड/ 4
